		\markbox{5341}{Let} \markbox{m5342}{$d_{2i}$} \markbox{5343}{be} \markbox{5344}{the} \markbox{m5345}{$2i$}-th \markbox{5346}{Betti} \markbox{5347}{number} \markbox{5348}{of} \markbox{5349}{a} \markbox{5350}{complex} \markbox{5351}{Grassmannian} \markbox{m5352}{$\mathbb CG_{n,k}$} \markbox{5353}{with} \markbox{m5354}{$d=k(n-k)$} \markbox{5355}{even.} \markbox{5356}{Then} \markbox{5357}{the} \markbox{5358}{sum} \markbox{m5359}{\(\sum _{i=0}^d d_{2i}\lambda^i\neq 0,\, \forall \lambda \in \mathbb Q.\)}
	\end{lemma}
	\begin{proof}
		\markbox{5360}{Let} \markbox{5361}{us} \markbox{5362}{consider} \markbox{5363}{the} \markbox{5364}{sum} \markbox{m5365}{$\sum_{i=0}^d d_{2i}\lambda^i$}, \markbox{5366}{when} \markbox{m5367}{$\lambda$} \markbox{5368}{is} \markbox{5369}{an} \markbox{5370}{integer.} 
		\markbox{5371}{Clearly,} $$\sum_{i=0}^d d_{2i}\lambda^i \equiv 1 \pmod{\lambda}.$$ %(see Theorem 2 in \cite{glover-homer}). 
		Hence, \markbox{m5372}{$\sum_{i=0}^d d_{2i}\lambda^i \neq 0$}, \markbox{5373}{if} \markbox{m5374}{$\lambda \neq \pm 1$}. \markbox{5375}{When} \markbox{m5376}{$\lambda = 1$}, \markbox{5377}{the} \markbox{5378}{sum} \markbox{5379}{is} \markbox{5380}{also} \markbox{5381}{positive} \markbox{5382}{and} \markbox{5383}{therefore} \markbox{5384}{nonzero.} \markbox{5385}{It} \markbox{5386}{remains} \markbox{5387}{to} \markbox{5388}{consider} \markbox{5389}{the} \markbox{5390}{case} \markbox{5391}{where} \markbox{m5392}{$\lambda = -1$}.
		\markbox{5393}{Let} \markbox{m5394}{$\chi(\mathbb{R}G_{n,k})$} \markbox{5395}{denote} \markbox{5396}{the} Euler-Poincar{\'e} \markbox{5397}{characteristic} \markbox{5398}{of} \markbox{m5399}{$\mathbb{R}G_{n,k}$} \markbox{5400}{and} \markbox{5401}{be} \markbox{5402}{defined} \markbox{5403}{by} $$\chi(X):=\sum_{i\ge0}\dim H^i(\mathbb{R}G_{n,k};\mathbb{Z}_2)$$ \markbox{5404}{where} \markbox{m5405}{$\mathbb{R}G_{n,k}$} \markbox{5406}{denotes} \markbox{5407}{the} \markbox{5408}{Grassmannian} \markbox{5409}{of} \markbox{5410}{real} \markbox{m5411}{$k$}-planes \markbox{5412}{in} \markbox{m5413}{$\mathbb{R}^n$}.
		\markbox{5414}{Now} \markbox{5415}{we} \markbox{5416}{observe} \markbox{5417}{that} 
		\markbox{m5418}{$\sum_{i=0}^d d_{2i}(-1)^i = \chi(\mathbb{R}G_{n,k})$} \markbox{5419}{where} \markbox{m5420}{$d_{2i} = \operatorname{dim} H^{2i}(\mathbb{C}G_{n,k}; \mathbb{Q}) = \dim H^{i}(\mathbb{R}G_{n,k}; \mathbb{Z}_2)$}. 
		\markbox{5421}{It} \markbox{5422}{is} \markbox{5423}{a} \markbox{5424}{well} \markbox{5425}{known} \markbox{5426}{fact} \markbox{5427}{that} \markbox{m5428}{$\chi(\mathbb{R}G_{n,k}) \neq 0$} \markbox{5429}{if} \markbox{m5430}{$k(n-k)$} \markbox{5431}{is} \markbox{5432}{even.} 
		
		\markbox{5433}{Let} \markbox{5434}{us} \markbox{5435}{move} \markbox{5436}{to} \markbox{5437}{the} \markbox{5438}{other} \markbox{5439}{case} \markbox{5440}{where} \markbox{m5441}{$\lambda\in \mathbb{Q}\backslash \mathbb{Z}$}. \markbox{5442}{Suppose} \markbox{m5443}{$\sum_{i=0}^{d} d_{2i}\lambda^i =0$} \markbox{5444}{for} \markbox{5445}{some} \markbox{m5446}{$\lambda = \frac{p}{q}$} \markbox{5447}{where} \markbox{m5448}{$p$} \markbox{5449}{and} \markbox{m5450}{$q$} \markbox{5451}{are} \markbox{5452}{coprime} \markbox{5453}{integers.} \markbox{5454}{Since} \markbox{m5455}{$d_0 =d_d =1$}, \markbox{5456}{using} \markbox{5457}{the} \markbox{5458}{rational} \markbox{5459}{root} \markbox{5460}{theorem} \markbox{m5461}{$p|1$} \markbox{5462}{and} \markbox{m5463}{$q|1$}. \markbox{5464}{Hence,} \markbox{m5465}{$\lambda = \pm 1$}, \markbox{5466}{which} \markbox{5467}{is} \markbox{5468}{a} \markbox{5469}{contradiction.} \markbox{5470}{Therefore,} \markbox{5471}{we} \markbox{5472}{conclude} \markbox{5473}{that} \markbox{m5474}{$\sum_{i=0}^{d} d_{2i}\lambda^i \neq 0$} \markbox{5475}{for} \markbox{5476}{all} \markbox{m5477}{$\lambda\in \mathbb Q$}. 
		%Thus, the sum  $\sum _{i=1}^d d_{2i}\lambda^i$ is nonzero for every integer value of $\lambda.$ 
		\iffalse	Now, \markbox{5478}{suppose} \markbox{5479}{for} \markbox{5480}{contradiction} \markbox{5481}{that} \markbox{5482}{there} \markbox{5483}{exists} \markbox{5484}{a} \markbox{5485}{rational} \markbox{5486}{number} \markbox{m5487}{$\lambda = a/b$}  \markbox{5488}{written} \markbox{5489}{in} \markbox{5490}{lowest} \markbox{5491}{terms} \markbox{5492}{(i.e.,} \markbox{m5493}{$\gcd(a,b)=1$}) \markbox{5494}{such} \markbox{5495}{that} \markbox{5496}{the} \markbox{5497}{sum} \markbox{5498}{vanishes.} \markbox{5499}{Note} \markbox{5500}{that} \markbox{5501}{in} \markbox{5502}{the} \markbox{5503}{polynomial} \markbox{m5504}{$\sum_{i=0}^{d} d_{2i}\lambda^i$}, \markbox{5505}{both} \markbox{5506}{the} \markbox{5507}{leading} \markbox{5508}{coefficient} \markbox{m5509}{$d_d$} \markbox{5510}{and} \markbox{5511}{the} \markbox{5512}{constant} \markbox{5513}{term} \markbox{m5514}{$d_0$} \markbox{5515}{are} \markbox{5516}{equal} \markbox{5517}{to} \markbox{m5518}{$1$}. \markbox{5519}{By} \markbox{5520}{the} \markbox{5521}{Rational} \markbox{5522}{Root} \markbox{5523}{Theorem,} \markbox{5524}{the} \markbox{5525}{rational} \markbox{5526}{root} \markbox{m5527}{$\lambda = a/b$} \markbox{5528}{must} \markbox{5529}{satisfy} \markbox{m5530}{$a \mid 1$} \markbox{5531}{and} \markbox{m5532}{$b \mid 1$}, \markbox{5533}{hence} \markbox{m5534}{$\lambda = \pm 1\in \mathbb Z$}. \markbox{5535}{Since} \markbox{5536}{this} \markbox{5537}{is} \markbox{5538}{not} \markbox{5539}{possible,} \fi
	\end{proof}
	
	
	
	\markbox{5540}{Denote} \markbox{5541}{the} \markbox{m5542}{$i$}-th \markbox{5543}{homology} \markbox{5544}{groups} 
	\markbox{m5545}{$H_i(\mathbb{C}G_{n,k}; \mathbb{Q}), \, H_i(\mathbb{S}^m; \mathbb{Q})$} \markbox{5546}{and} 
	\markbox{m5547}{$H_i(\mathbb{S}^m \times \mathbb{C}G_{n,k}; \mathbb{Q})$}, \markbox{5548}{by} \markbox{m5549}{$H_i^{\mathbb{C}G}, H_i^{\mathbb{S}}$} \markbox{5550}{and} \markbox{m5551}{$H_i^{\times}$}, \markbox{5552}{respectively.} \markbox{5553}{Let} \markbox{m5554}{$d$} \markbox{5555}{denote} \markbox{5556}{the} \markbox{5557}{complex} \markbox{5558}{dimension} \markbox{5559}{of} \markbox{m5560}{$\mathbb CG_{n,k}$}, \markbox{5561}{given} \markbox{5562}{by} \markbox{m5563}{$d = k(n - k)$}. \markbox{5564}{Then} \markbox{5565}{we} \markbox{5566}{have} \markbox{5567}{the} \markbox{5568}{following} proposition.
	\begin{proposition}\label{CP of CGnk}
		\markbox{5569}{Consider} \markbox{5570}{a} \markbox{5571}{complex} \markbox{5572}{Grassmannian} \markbox{m5573}{$\mathbb{C}G_{n,k}$} \markbox{5574}{such} \markbox{5575}{that} \markbox{5576}{the} \markbox{5577}{hypothesis} \eqref{Homer} \markbox{5578}{is} \markbox{5579}{satisfied} \markbox{5580}{and} \markbox{m5581}{$k(n-k)$} \markbox{5582}{is} \markbox{5583}{even.} \markbox{5584}{Let} \markbox{m5585}{$g $} \markbox{5586}{be} \markbox{5587}{a} \markbox{5588}{continuous} \markbox{5589}{map} \markbox{5590}{on} \markbox{m5591}{$\mathbb{C}G_{n,k}$} \markbox{5592}{with} \markbox{5593}{nonzero} \markbox{5594}{Brouwer} \markbox{5595}{degree.} \markbox{5596}{Then} \markbox{5597}{the} \markbox{5598}{pair} \markbox{m5599}{$(\mathbb{C}G_{n,k}, g)$} \markbox{5600}{has} \markbox{5601}{the} \markbox{5602}{coincidence} property.
	\end{proposition}
	
	
	\begin{proof}
	\markbox{5603}{Self-maps} \markbox{5604}{with} \markbox{5605}{nonzero} \markbox{5606}{Brouwer} \markbox{5607}{degree} \markbox{5608}{induces} \markbox{5609}{automorphisms} \markbox{5610}{in} \markbox{5611}{the} \markbox{5612}{rational} \markbox{5613}{cohomology} \markbox{5614}{algebra.} \markbox{5615}{Using} \markbox{5616}{Theorem} \ref{hom and hof} \markbox{5617}{part} \markbox{5618}{\textit{(i)}}, \markbox{5619}{there} \markbox{5620}{exist} \markbox{5621}{a} \markbox{5622}{nonzero} \markbox{5623}{rational} \markbox{m5624}{$\lambda$} \markbox{5625}{such} \markbox{5626}{that} \markbox{m5627}{$g^*(c_i)=\lambda^ic_i, \forall i\in I.$} \markbox{5628}{Let} \markbox{m5629}{$f$} \markbox{5630}{be} \markbox{5631}{a} \markbox{5632}{continuous} \markbox{5633}{map} \markbox{5634}{on} \markbox{m5635}{$\mathbb CG_{n,k}$} \markbox{5636}{and} \markbox{5637}{using} \thmref{hom and hof} \markbox{5638}{part} \markbox{5639}{\textit{(i)}}, \markbox{5640}{there} \markbox{5641}{exists} \markbox{m5642}{$\mu \in \mathbb Q$} \markbox{5643}{such} that
		\[
		f^*(c_i)=\mu^ic_i, \forall i\in I.
		\]
		\markbox{5644}{Then} \markbox{5645}{by} \markbox{5646}{the} \markbox{5647}{Universal} \markbox{5648}{Coefficient} \markbox{5649}{Theorem,} \markbox{m5650}{$ \hom_{\mathbb{Q}} (H_i^{\mathbb CG};\mathbb Q) \cong H^i_{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{5651}{non-canonically} \markbox{5652}{which} \markbox{5653}{implies} \markbox{5654}{that} 
		\begin{align*}
			\varphi \circ f_* &= f^*(\varphi) , \, \forall
			\varphi \in \hom _{\mathbb Q}\big(H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}, \mathbb Q\big)\cong H^{2i}_{\mathbb CG}.\\
			\varphi(f_*(x))&=(f^*(\varphi))(x)= \mu^i\varphi(x)=\varphi(\mu^ix),\; \forall x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}.
		\end{align*}
		\markbox{5655}{The} \markbox{5656}{last} \markbox{5657}{equation} \markbox{5658}{implies} \markbox{5659}{that} \markbox{m5660}{$f_*(x)=\mu^ix,\, \forall x\in  H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}.$}
		%This implies for all $\varphi\in \hom_{\mathbb Q}(H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG},\mathbb Q)$ and $x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}$, we have
		Now \markbox{5661}{observe} \markbox{5662}{that} \markbox{m5663}{$D\circ g^*\circ D^{-1}\circ f_*: H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}\to H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{5664}{is} \markbox{5665}{given} \markbox{5666}{by} 
		\[
		D\circ g^*\circ D^{-1}\circ f_*(x)=D\circ g^*\circ D^{-1}(\mu^ix)=\mu^iD\circ g^*(D^{-1}x)=\mu^iD(\lambda^{d-i}D^{-1}x)=\mu^i\lambda^{d-i}x.
		\]
		\markbox{5667}{Thus} \markbox{5668}{for} \markbox{m5669}{$x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$}, \markbox{5670}{the} \markbox{5671}{Lefschetz} \markbox{5672}{coincidence} \markbox{5673}{number} \markbox{5674}{is} \markbox{5675}{given} by
		\[
		\begin{array}{ll}
			L(f,g) &= \sum_{i=0}^d (-1)^{2i}
			\mathrm{tr}(D\circ g^*\circ D^{-1}\circ f_*(x)) \\[6pt]
			&=  \sum_{i=0}^d d_{2i}\mu^i\lambda^{d-i}  \\[6pt]
			&= \lambda^d \sum_{i=0}^d d_{2i}(\mu/\lambda)^i \neq 0 \quad (\because \lambda\neq 0) 
		\end{array}
		\]
		\markbox{5676}{where} \markbox{m5677}{$d_{2i}$} \markbox{5678}{denotes} \markbox{m5679}{$\dim_{\mathbb Q}H^{2i}_{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{5680}{and} \markbox{5681}{the} \markbox{5682}{last} \markbox{5683}{equation} \markbox{5684}{holds} \markbox{5685}{by} \markbox{5686}{using} \lemref{sum neq 0}. \markbox{5687}{Therefore,} \markbox{5688}{using} \thmref{LCT} \markbox{5689}{the} \markbox{5690}{pair} \markbox{m5691}{$(\mathbb{C}G_{n,k},g)$} \markbox{5692}{has} \markbox{5693}{the} \markbox{5694}{coincidence} property.
	\end{proof}
	
	\iffalse{}  \textcolor{teal}{
		In the case of a quaternionic Grassmannian $\mathbb H G_{n,k}$, an Adams operation of degree $-1$ cannot be induced by any self-map, since its action on $H^*(\mathbb H G_{n,k};\mathbb Z/3)$ does not commute with the reduced third power operation (see Theorem~2(2) of \cite{glover-homer}). Consequently, the value $\lambda=-1$ cannot occur in the sum $\sum_{i=0}^{d} d_{2i}\lambda^i$ from Lemma~\ref{sum neq 0}, so the sum is nonzero in all cases, regardless of the parity of $d=k(n-k)$. Proceeding as in Proposition~\ref{CP of CGnk}, one obtains the following extension of Theorem~2(2) in \cite{glover-homer}:
		\begin{proposition}\label{CP of HGnk}
			For any homotopy equivalence $g$ of a quaternionic Grassmannian $\mathbb H G_{n,k}$, the pair $(\mathbb H G_{n,k},g)$ has the coincidence property.
		\end{proposition}
	}
	\fi
	
	
	
	
	\subsection{} \markbox{5695}{Denote} \markbox{5696}{by} \markbox{m5697}{$H_*^\times = \bigoplus_{i\geq 0} H_i^{\times},\, H_*^{\mathbb{C}G} = \bigoplus_{i\geq 0} H_i^{\mathbb{C}G},\, H_*^{\mathbb{S}} = \bigoplus_{i\geq 0} H_i^{\mathbb{S}}$} \markbox{5698}{and} \markbox{m5699}{$\vartheta$} \markbox{5700}{the} \markbox{5701}{fundamental} \markbox{5702}{class} \markbox{m5703}{$[\mathbb S^m]\in H_m^{\mathbb S}$}. \markbox{5704}{Let} \markbox{m5705}{$\{v_q\}$} \markbox{5706}{be} \markbox{5707}{a} \markbox{5708}{homogeneous} \markbox{5709}{basis} \markbox{5710}{of} \markbox{m5711}{$H_*^{\mathbb{C}G}$}, \markbox{5712}{and} \markbox{5713}{let} \markbox{m5714}{$\{\delta_{v_q}\}$} \markbox{5715}{denote} \markbox{5716}{the} \markbox{5717}{corresponding} \markbox{5718}{dual} \markbox{5719}{basis} \markbox{5720}{of}  
	\markbox{m5721}{$\operatorname{Hom}(H_*^{\mathbb{C}G}, \mathbb Q) \cong H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}$}, \markbox{5722}{such} \markbox{5723}{that}  
	\markbox{m5724}{$ \delta_{v_q} (v_p) = \delta_{qp}$} \markbox{5725}{where} \markbox{m5726}{$\delta_{qp}$} \markbox{5727}{is} \markbox{5728}{the} \markbox{5729}{Kronecker} \markbox{5730}{delta} \markbox{5731}{function.} \markbox{5732}{Without} \markbox{5733}{loss} \markbox{5734}{of} \markbox{5735}{generality,} \markbox{5736}{assume} \markbox{5737}{that} \markbox{m5738}{$1=v_0 \in \{v_i\}$} \markbox{5739}{represents} \markbox{5740}{the} \markbox{5741}{generator} \markbox{5742}{of} \markbox{m5743}{$H_0^{\mathbb{C}G} \cong \mathbb Q$}.
	
	\markbox{5744}{Over} \markbox{m5745}{$\mathbb Q$}, \markbox{5746}{the} K\"unneth \markbox{5747}{Theorem} \markbox{5748}{yields} \markbox{5749}{the} \markbox{5750}{following} \markbox{5751}{decompositions} 
	\iffalse	Set \markbox{m5752}{$d = 2k(n - k)$}, \markbox{m5753}{$m=2s$} \markbox{5754}{and} \markbox{m5755}{$t={n \choose k}$}. 
	
	\markbox{5756}{By} Remark~\ref{lift}, \markbox{5757}{every} \markbox{5758}{continuous} \markbox{5759}{map} \markbox{m5760}{$f$} \markbox{5761}{on} \markbox{m5762}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{5763}{admits} \markbox{5764}{a} \markbox{5765}{lift} 
	\markbox{m5766}{$\tilde f$} \markbox{5767}{on} \markbox{m5768}{$\mathbb{S}^m \times \mathbb{C}G_{n,k}$} \markbox{5769}{satisfying} 
	\markbox{m5770}{$f \circ \pi = \pi \circ \tilde f,$}
	\markbox{5771}{where} \markbox{m5772}{$\pi : \mathbb{S}^m \times \mathbb{C}G_{n,k} \to P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{5773}{is} \markbox{5774}{the} \markbox{5775}{double} \markbox{5776}{covering} \markbox{5777}{map.} 
	\markbox{5778}{We} \markbox{5779}{continue} \markbox{5780}{to} \markbox{5781}{denote} \markbox{5782}{such} \markbox{5783}{lifts} \markbox{5784}{by} \markbox{5785}{the} \markbox{5786}{corresponding} \markbox{5787}{maps} \markbox{5788}{on} \markbox{m5789}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{5790}{with} \markbox{5791}{a} tilde.
	\markbox{5792}{By} Theorem~\ref{main thm}, \markbox{5793}{there} \markbox{5794}{exists}  \markbox{m5795}{$\lambda \in \mathbb{Q}$} \markbox{5796}{or} \markbox{m5797}{$P_i\in H^{2i-m}_{\mathbb CG} \;\forall i\in I$} \markbox{5798}{with} \markbox{5799}{some} \markbox{m5800}{$P_i\neq 0$}, \markbox{5801}{such} \markbox{5802}{that} \
	
	\begin{equation}
		\text{either (i) } 
		\tilde f^*(c_i) = \lambda^i c_i,\forall i\in I, \text{or (ii) } \tilde f^*(c_i)=uP_i, \  \forall i\in I , 
	\end{equation}
	\begin{equation}
		\text{and either (iii) }\tilde f^*(u) = \mu u \text{ for some }\mu\in \mathbb Q, \text{or (iv) }\tilde f^*(u) \in H^m_{\mathbb{C}G}.
	\end{equation}
	
	
	%We have the induced maps in homology and cohomology $\tilde f_*$ and $\tilde f^*$, respectively, related by the Kronecker pairing 
	%$\langle \;,\;\rangle:H^i_\times\times H_i^\times\to \mathbb Q$ defined by
	%\[
	%\langle \tilde f^* \varphi, x\rangle = \langle \varphi, \tilde f_* x\rangle 
	%\quad \text{for all } \varphi \in H^i_\times,\, x \in H_i^\times.
	%\]
	%and $u \in H^*_\times$ corresponds to the fundamental class 
	%of $[\mathbb S^m] \in H^{\mathbb S}_m \subseteq H^\times_m.$
	
	%Fix a basis $\{1, v_1, v_2, \ldots, v_t\}$ for $H_*^{\mathbb{C}G}$. 
	%The corresponding dual basis of $\hom(H_*^{\mathbb{C}G
		%}, \mathbb{Q}) \cong H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}$ is 
	%$\{\delta_1, \delta_{v_1}, \delta_{v_2}, \ldots, \delta_{v_t}\}$, 
	%where \ $\delta_{v_i}(x) = \langle \delta_{v_i}, x \rangle$ defined to be $1$ if and only if $x=v_i$, and $0$ otherwise, for all $v_i$.
	\fi  
	\begin{equation}\label{kunneth}
		H_i^\times \cong H_i^{\mathbb{C}G} \oplus (\vartheta \otimes H_{i-m}^{\mathbb{C}G}), 
		\qquad 
		H^i_\times \cong H^i_{\mathbb{C}G} \oplus uH^{i-m}_{\mathbb{C}G},
	\end{equation}
	\markbox{5803}{where}  \markbox{m5804}{$u \in H^m_{\times} \cong \operatorname{Hom}(H_m^{\times}, \mathbb Q)$} \markbox{5805}{corresponds} \markbox{5806}{to} \markbox{5807}{the} \markbox{5808}{element} \markbox{m5809}{$\delta_{\vartheta\otimes 1}$}.
	
	
	\markbox{5810}{Using} \eqref{kunneth}, \markbox{5811}{we} \markbox{5812}{can} \markbox{5813}{extend} \markbox{5814}{the} \markbox{5815}{chosen} \markbox{5816}{basis} \markbox{m5817}{$\{v_q\}$} \markbox{5818}{of} \markbox{m5819}{$H_*^{\mathbb{C}G}$} \markbox{5820}{to} \markbox{m5821}{$	\{v_q\} \cup \{\vartheta \otimes v_q\}$} \markbox{5822}{of} \markbox{m5823}{$H_*^\times$} \markbox{5824}{such} \markbox{5825}{that} \markbox{5826}{the} \markbox{5827}{corresponding} \markbox{5828}{dual} \markbox{5829}{basis} \markbox{5830}{can} \markbox{5831}{also} \markbox{5832}{be} \markbox{5833}{extended} \markbox{5834}{from} \markbox{m5835}{$\{\delta_{v_q}\}$} \markbox{5836}{of} \markbox{m5837}{$ \hom (H_*^{\mathbb{C}G};\mathbb{Q})$} \markbox{5838}{to} \markbox{m5839}{$\{\delta_{v_q}\} \cup \{\delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_q}\} $} \markbox{5840}{of} \markbox{m5841}{$\hom (H_*^{\times};\mathbb{Q})$} satisfying:
	%\[\{v_i\} \cup \{\vartheta \otimes v_i\} \subseteq H_*^\times, \qquad 	\{\delta_{v_i}\} \cup \{\delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_i}\} \subseteq H^*_\times.\]
	%Since $\delta_{U \otimes 1} = \delta_U = u \in H^m_{\mathbb S}$, we write $\delta_{U \otimes v_i}$ simply as $u\,\delta_{v_i}$.With respect to these bases, the Kronecker pairing  $\langle\,\cdot\,,\cdot\,\rangle : H^*_\times \times H_*^\times \longrightarrow \mathbb Q$satisfies 
	\begin{equation}\label{Kronecker relations}
		\delta_{v_q}( v_p) = \delta_{qp}, \quad
		\delta_{v_q}( \vartheta \otimes v_p)= 0, \quad
		\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_q}(v_p) = 0, \quad
		\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_q}(\vartheta \otimes v_p)= \delta_{qp}.
	\end{equation}
	%since $\langle u, \vartheta\rangle=1$ and $u$ (resp. $\vartheta$) kills the other basis elements.Thus the matrix of the pairing in these bases is the identity, hence the  map$\kappa_i: H^i_\times \to \operatorname{Hom}(H_i^\times,\mathbb Q)$, $\kappa_i(\varphi)(x)=\langle \varphi, x\rangle$, is an isomorphism for all $i$. 
	Let \markbox{m5842}{$f$} \markbox{5843}{be} \markbox{5844}{a} \markbox{5845}{continuous} \markbox{5846}{function} \markbox{5847}{on} \markbox{m5848}{$P(m,n,k)$}. \markbox{5849}{Using} \remref{lift} \markbox{5850}{and} \markbox{5851}{the} \markbox{5852}{Universal} \markbox{5853}{Coefficient} \markbox{5854}{Theorem,} \markbox{5855}{there} \markbox{5856}{exist} \markbox{5857}{a} \markbox{5858}{lift} \markbox{m5859}{$\tilde{f}$} \markbox{5860}{on} \markbox{m5861}{$\mathbb{S}^m\times \mathbb{C}G_{n,k}$} \markbox{5862}{satisfying} \begin{equation}\label{comm with phi}
		\varphi \circ \tilde{f}_* = \tilde{f}^*(\varphi) , \, \forall
		\varphi \in \hom _{\mathbb Q}\big(H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}, \mathbb Q\big)\cong H^{2i}_{\mathbb CG}.
	\end{equation}
	
		Poincar\'e \markbox{5863}{duality} \markbox{5864}{on} \markbox{m5865}{$\mathbb S^{m}\times \mathbb C G_{n,k}$} \markbox{5866}{can} \markbox{5867}{be} \markbox{5868}{described} \markbox{5869}{in} \markbox{5870}{terms} \markbox{5871}{of} \markbox{5872}{the} \markbox{5873}{duality} \markbox{5874}{on} \markbox{5875}{the} \markbox{5876}{Grassmannian} \markbox{5877}{factor.} \markbox{5878}{Let} 
		\markbox{m5879}{$D_{\mathbb C G}\colon H^{i}_{\mathbb C G}\to H_{2d-i}^{\mathbb C G}$} 
		\markbox{5880}{be} \markbox{5881}{the} Poincar\'e \markbox{5882}{duality} \markbox{5883}{isomorphism} \markbox{5884}{defined} \markbox{5885}{in} \eqref{poinc dua} \markbox{5886}{for} \markbox{m5887}{$\mathbb C G_{n,k}$}, \markbox{5888}{where} \markbox{m5889}{$d=k(n-k)$}.  
		\markbox{5890}{The} Poincar\'e \markbox{5891}{duality} \markbox{5892}{isomorphism} \markbox{5893}{on} \markbox{5894}{the} product
		\markbox{5895}{is} \markbox{5896}{then} \markbox{5897}{determined} \markbox{5898}{on} \markbox{5899}{the} \markbox{5900}{basis} \markbox{5901}{elements} \markbox{5902}{by}  
		\begin{equation}
			D\colon H^{j}_{\times}\to H_{m+2d-j}^{\times}, \quad \delta_{v_i}\mapsto \vartheta\otimes D_{\mathbb C G}(\delta_{v_i})\quad\text{and}\quad \delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_i} \mapsto D_{\mathbb C G}(\delta_{v_i}).
		\end{equation}
		\markbox{5903}{We} \markbox{5904}{are} \markbox{5905}{now} \markbox{5906}{ready} \markbox{5907}{to} \markbox{5908}{establish} \markbox{5909}{the} \markbox{5910}{following} \markbox{5911}{lemmas,} \markbox{5912}{which} \markbox{5913}{will} \markbox{5914}{be} \markbox{5915}{useful} \markbox{5916}{in} \markbox{5917}{the} sequel.
	\begin{lemma}\label{image of homf}
		\markbox{5918}{Let} \markbox{m5919}{$f$} \markbox{5920}{be} \markbox{5921}{a} \markbox{5922}{continuous} \markbox{5923}{function} \markbox{5924}{on} \markbox{m5925}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{5926}{and} \markbox{m5927}{$\tilde{f}$} \markbox{5928}{be} \markbox{5929}{the} \markbox{5930}{lift} \markbox{5931}{defined} \markbox{5932}{in} \remref{lift} \markbox{5933}{such} \markbox{5934}{that} \markbox{m5935}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_1)\neq au,\, a\in \mathbb{Q}$} \markbox{5936}{and} \markbox{m5937}{$k<n-k$}. \markbox{5938}{Then} \markbox{5939}{there} \markbox{5940}{exist} \markbox{m5941}{$\lambda \in \mathbb{Q}\backslash \{0\}$} \markbox{5942}{and} \markbox{m5943}{$\mu \in \mathbb{Q}$} \markbox{5944}{such} \markbox{5945}{that} \markbox{5946}{the} \markbox{5947}{induced} \markbox{5948}{map} \markbox{m5949}{$\tilde{f}_*$} \markbox{5950}{on} \markbox{m5951}{$H_*^{\times}$} \markbox{5952}{is} \markbox{5953}{of} \markbox{5954}{the} \markbox{5955}{following} form.
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item {} Either \markbox{m5956}{$\tilde{f}_*(\vartheta\otimes x) = \mu \lambda^i (\vartheta \otimes x),\, \forall x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$} \markbox{5957}{or} \markbox{m5958}{$\tilde{f}_*(\vartheta\otimes x) \in H_*^{\mathbb{CG}},\, \forall x \in H_*^{\mathbb{C}G}$}.
			\item {} \markbox{m5959}{$\tilde{f}_*(x) = \lambda^i x + \vartheta\otimes y,$} \markbox{5960}{for} \markbox{5961}{some} \markbox{m5962}{$y \in H_{2i-m}^{\mathbb{C}G}, \, \forall x \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}.$}
		\end{enumerate}
		\markbox{5963}{Moreover,} \markbox{m5964}{$y=0$} \markbox{5965}{in} \markbox{5966}{\textit{(2)}} \markbox{5967}{if} \markbox{m5968}{$\tilde{f}_*(\vartheta\otimes x) = \mu \lambda^i (\vartheta \otimes x),\, \forall x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$}.
	\end{lemma}
	\begin{proof}
		\markbox{5969}{Using} \thmref{main thm}, \markbox{5970}{there} \markbox{5971}{exist} \markbox{m5972}{$\lambda \in \mathbb{Q}\backslash \{0\}$} \markbox{5973}{such} \markbox{5974}{that} \markbox{m5975}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_i) = \lambda^i c_i, \forall i \in I$} \markbox{5976}{and} \markbox{5977}{either} \markbox{m5978}{$\tilde{f}^*(u) = \mu u,\, \mu \in \mathbb{Q}$} \markbox{5979}{or} \markbox{m5980}{$\tilde{f}^*(u)\in H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}$}. \markbox{5981}{It} \markbox{5982}{is} \markbox{5983}{sufficient} \markbox{5984}{to} \markbox{5985}{prove} \markbox{5986}{the} \markbox{5987}{result} \markbox{5988}{for} \markbox{5989}{the} \markbox{5990}{chosen} \markbox{5991}{basis} \markbox{m5992}{$\{v_q\}\cup\{\vartheta\otimes v_q\}$} \markbox{5993}{of} \markbox{m5994}{$H_{*}^{\times}$}. 
		
		\markbox{5995}{Let} \markbox{5996}{us} \markbox{5997}{consider} \markbox{5998}{the} \markbox{5999}{first} \markbox{6000}{case} \markbox{6001}{where} \markbox{m6002}{$\tilde{f}^*(u) = \mu u$}. \markbox{6003}{Using} \markbox{m6004}{$H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}\cong \hom(H_*^{\mathbb{C}G},\mathbb{Q})$}, \markbox{6005}{we} \markbox{6006}{have} \begin{equation}\label{fstarco}
			\tilde{f}^*(\delta_{v_p}) = \lambda^i \delta_{v_{p}}, \, \forall v_{p}\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}, \quad \tilde{f}^*(\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_{p}})  = \mu \lambda^i (\delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_{p}}), \, \forall v_{p}\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}.
		\end{equation}
		\markbox{6007}{If} \markbox{m6008}{$m$} \markbox{6009}{is} \markbox{6010}{odd,} \markbox{6011}{then} \markbox{6012}{the} \markbox{6013}{coefficient} \markbox{6014}{of} \markbox{6015}{any} \markbox{6016}{basis} \markbox{6017}{element} \markbox{m6018}{$v_p \in H_*^{\mathbb{C}G}$} \markbox{6019}{in} \markbox{m6020}{$\tilde{f}_*(\vartheta \otimes v_q)$} \markbox{6021}{and} \markbox{m6022}{$\vartheta \otimes v_p$} \markbox{6023}{in} \markbox{m6024}{$\tilde{f}_*(v_q)$} \markbox{6025}{is} \markbox{6026}{zero} \markbox{6027}{because} \markbox{m6028}{$\tilde{f}_*$} \markbox{6029}{is} \markbox{6030}{a} \markbox{6031}{graded} \markbox{6032}{map.} \markbox{6033}{Let} \markbox{6034}{us} \markbox{6035}{consider} \markbox{6036}{the} \markbox{6037}{case} \markbox{6038}{where} \markbox{m6039}{$m=2s$}.
		\markbox{6040}{By} \eqref{comm with phi} \markbox{6041}{and} \eqref{fstarco}, \markbox{6042}{the} \markbox{6043}{coefficient} \markbox{6044}{of} \markbox{6045}{a} \markbox{6046}{basis} \markbox{6047}{element} \markbox{m6048}{$v_p\in H_{2i+m}^{\mathbb{C}G}$} \markbox{6049}{in} \markbox{m6050}{$\tilde{f}_*(\vartheta \otimes v_q)$} \markbox{6051}{written} \markbox{6052}{as} \markbox{6053}{a} \markbox{m6054}{$\mathbb{Q}$}-linear \markbox{6055}{combination} \markbox{6056}{of} \markbox{6057}{the} \markbox{6058}{basis} \markbox{6059}{elements} \markbox{6060}{from} \markbox{m6061}{$\{v_q\}\cup\{\vartheta\otimes v_q\}$} \markbox{6062}{is} \markbox{6063}{the} following:
		$$	 \delta_{v_p}\circ \tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q)
		=  \tilde f^* (\delta_{v_p}) (\vartheta\otimes v_q)
		=  \lambda^{i+s} \delta_{v_p}(\vartheta\otimes v_q)
		= 0,\, \forall v_q \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$$
		\markbox{6064}{and} \markbox{6065}{the} \markbox{6066}{coefficient} \markbox{6067}{of} \markbox{6068}{a} \markbox{6069}{basis} \markbox{6070}{element} \markbox{m6071}{$\vartheta \otimes v_p\in \vartheta \otimes H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$} \markbox{6072}{in} \markbox{m6073}{$\tilde{f}_*(\vartheta \otimes v_q)$} is
		$$ \delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p}\circ \tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q)
		=  \tilde f^*(\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p})(\vartheta\otimes v_q)
		=  \mu \lambda^{i}\;\delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_p}(\vartheta\otimes v_q)= \mu\lambda^{i}\delta_{pq},\, \forall v_q \in H^{\mathbb{C}G}_{2i}.$$
		\markbox{6074}{This} \markbox{6075}{implies} \markbox{6076}{that} $$\tilde{f}_*(\vartheta \otimes v_q) = \mu \lambda^i (\vartheta \otimes v_q), \, \forall v_q \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}.$$ 
		\markbox{6077}{Using} \markbox{6078}{similar} \markbox{6079}{calculations} \markbox{6080}{given} \markbox{6081}{above,} \markbox{6082}{it} \markbox{6083}{is} \markbox{6084}{easy} \markbox{6085}{to} \markbox{6086}{show} \markbox{6087}{that} $$\delta_{v_p}\circ \tilde{f}_*(v_q) = \lambda^i \delta_{pq},\, \forall v_q \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G},\quad \delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_p}\circ \tilde{f}_*(v_q)=0,\, \forall v_q\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}.$$ \markbox{6088}{Therefore,} \markbox{m6089}{$\tilde{f}_*(v_q) = \lambda^i v_q,\, \forall v_q \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$}.\\
		
		\markbox{6090}{If} \markbox{m6091}{$\tilde{f}^*(u)\in H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}$}. \markbox{6092}{Again} \markbox{6093}{using} \markbox{m6094}{$H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}\cong \hom(H_*^{\mathbb{C}G},\mathbb{Q})$}, \markbox{6095}{we} \markbox{6096}{have} \begin{equation}\label{second u}
			\tilde{f}^*(\delta_{v_p}) = \lambda^i \delta_{v_{p}}, \, \forall v_{p}\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}, \quad \tilde{f}^*(\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_{p}})  \in H^*_{\mathbb{C}G},\, \forall  v_{p}\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}.
		\end{equation}
		\markbox{6097}{By} \eqref{comm with phi} \markbox{6098}{and} \eqref{second u}, \markbox{6099}{we} \markbox{6100}{get} \markbox{m6101}{$\delta_{v_p}\circ \tilde{f}_*(v_q) = \lambda^i \delta_{pq},\, \forall v_q \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G},$} \markbox{6102}{which} \markbox{6103}{implies} \markbox{6104}{that} \markbox{m6105}{$\tilde{f}_*(x) = \lambda^i x + \vartheta\otimes y,$} \markbox{6106}{for} \markbox{6107}{some} \markbox{m6108}{$y \in H_{2i-m}^{\mathbb{C}G}, \, \forall x \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}.$} \markbox{6109}{Note} \markbox{6110}{that} \markbox{m6111}{$\tilde f^*(\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p})\in H_{\mathbb CG}^*$} \markbox{6112}{and} \markbox{6113}{equal} \markbox{6114}{to} \markbox{6115}{some} \markbox{m6116}{$\sum a_j\delta_{v_j}$}. \markbox{6117}{Then} 
		%coefficient of $\vartheta \otimes v_p $ in $\tilde f_*(\vartheta \otimes v_q)$ is 
		\begin{equation}\label{computation}
			\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p}\circ \tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q)= \tilde f^*(\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p})(\vartheta\otimes v_q)=\sum a_j\delta_{v_j}(\vartheta\otimes v_q)=0.
		\end{equation}
		\markbox{6118}{Hence,} \markbox{m6119}{$\tilde f_*(\vartheta \otimes v_q)\in H_*^{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{6120}{for} \markbox{6121}{all} \markbox{m6122}{$\vartheta \otimes v_q\in\vartheta\otimes H_*^{\mathbb CG} $}.
		%	$ \text{ or } \tilde{f}^*(\vartheta\otimes v_{p}) \in H_*^{\mathbb{C}G},\, \forall v_{p}\in H_*^{\mathbb{C}G}$
	\end{proof}
\iffalse	\begin{remark}\label{lemrem}
		\markbox{6123}{For} \markbox{6124}{the} \markbox{6125}{case} \markbox{m6126}{$k=n-k$} \markbox{6127}{in} \lemref{image of homf}, \markbox{6128}{if} \markbox{m6129}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_i) = \lambda^i c_i$} \markbox{6130}{then} \markbox{6131}{we} \markbox{6132}{will} \markbox{6133}{get} \markbox{6134}{the} \markbox{6135}{same} \markbox{6136}{result} \markbox{6137}{otherwise} \markbox{6138}{when} \markbox{m6139}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_i) = (-\lambda)^i c_i$} \markbox{6140}{then} \markbox{m6141}{$\lambda$} \markbox{6142}{will} \markbox{6143}{be} \markbox{6144}{replaced} \markbox{6145}{by} \markbox{m6146}{$-\lambda$} \markbox{6147}{in} \lemref{image of homf}. 
	\end{remark}\fi
	\begin{lemma}\label{image of homf under hom}
		\markbox{6148}{Assume} \markbox{6149}{that} \markbox{6150}{the} \markbox{6151}{hypothesis} \eqref{Homer} \markbox{6152}{is} \markbox{6153}{satisfied.} 	\markbox{6154}{Let} \markbox{m6155}{$f$} \markbox{6156}{be} \markbox{6157}{a} \markbox{6158}{continuous} \markbox{6159}{function} \markbox{6160}{on} \markbox{m6161}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{6162}{and} \markbox{m6163}{$\tilde{f}$} \markbox{6164}{be} \markbox{6165}{the} \markbox{6166}{lift} \markbox{6167}{defined} \markbox{6168}{in} \remref{lift} \markbox{6169}{such} \markbox{6170}{that} \markbox{m6171}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_1)= au,\, a\in \mathbb{Q}$}. \markbox{6172}{Then} \markbox{6173}{the} \markbox{6174}{induced} \markbox{6175}{map} \markbox{m6176}{$\tilde{f}_*$} \markbox{6177}{on} \markbox{m6178}{$H_{*}^{\times}$} \markbox{6179}{is} \markbox{6180}{of} \markbox{6181}{the} \markbox{6182}{following} form.
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item {} \markbox{m6183}{$\tilde f_* (x)\in \vartheta\otimes H_{2i-m}^{\mathbb CG},\, \forall x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG},\, \forall i>0$}.
			\item {} \markbox{m6184}{$\tilde{f}_*(\vartheta\otimes 1) = \mu (\vartheta\otimes 1 )+y, \, y\in H_{m}^{\mathbb{C}G}, \quad\\ \tilde f_*(\vartheta \otimes x)\in H_{2i+m}^{\mathbb{C}G},\, \forall x \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}, i>0\;$} \markbox{6185}{if} \markbox{m6186}{$\tilde{f}^*(u) = \mu u,\,  \mu \in \mathbb{Q}$} 
		\end{enumerate}
	\end{lemma}
	\begin{proof}
		\markbox{6187}{Using} \propref{main thm 2}, \markbox{6188}{we} \markbox{6189}{have} \markbox{m6190}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_i) = u P_i,$} \markbox{6191}{for} \markbox{6192}{some} \markbox{m6193}{$P_i\in H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}$} \markbox{6194}{and} \markbox{6195}{either} \markbox{m6196}{$\tilde{f}^*(u) = \mu u,\, \mu \in \mathbb{Q}$} \markbox{6197}{or} \markbox{m6198}{$\tilde{f}^*(u)\in H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}$}. \\
		\markbox{6199}{Let} \markbox{6200}{us} \markbox{6201}{consider} \markbox{6202}{the} \markbox{6203}{first} \markbox{6204}{case} \markbox{6205}{where} \markbox{m6206}{$\tilde{f}^*(u) = \mu u$}. \markbox{6207}{Using} \markbox{m6208}{$H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}\cong \hom(H_*^{\mathbb{C}G},\mathbb{Q})$}, \markbox{6209}{we} \markbox{6210}{have} \markbox{6211}{for} \markbox{m6212}{$i>0$} 
		\begin{equation}\label{fstarcom}
			\tilde{f}^*(\delta_{v_p}) = \sum a_{jp}\delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_j} , \, \forall v_{p}\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}, \quad \tilde{f}^*(\delta_{\vartheta\otimes 1})  =\mu \delta_{\vartheta \otimes 1}, \quad \tilde{f}^*(\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_{p}})  = 0, \, \forall v_{p}\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}.
		\end{equation}
		\markbox{6213}{Using} \eqref{comm with phi}, \eqref{fstarcom} \markbox{6214}{and} \markbox{6215}{similar} \markbox{6216}{calculations} \markbox{6217}{given} \markbox{6218}{in} \markbox{6219}{the} \markbox{6220}{proof} \markbox{6221}{of} \lemref{image of homf}, \markbox{6222}{we} \markbox{6223}{have} \markbox{6224}{for} \markbox{m6225}{$ v_p\neq 1$}
		$$\delta_{v_p}\circ \tilde{f}_*(v_q) = 0,\, \forall v_q \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G},\quad \delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p}\circ \tilde{f}_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q) =0,\, \forall v_q \in H_{2i}^{*}$$ \markbox{6226}{that} \markbox{6227}{concludes} \markbox{6228}{the} result.
		
		\markbox{6229}{When} \markbox{m6230}{$\tilde{f}^*(u)\in H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}$} \markbox{6231}{then} \markbox{6232}{also} \markbox{6233}{we} \markbox{6234}{have} \markbox{m6235}{$\tilde{f}^*(\delta_{v_p}) = \sum a_{jp}\delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_j} , \, \forall v_{p}\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G},\, \forall i>0$} \markbox{6236}{which} \markbox{6237}{implies} \markbox{6238}{that} \markbox{m6239}{$\delta_{v_p}\circ \tilde{f}_*(v_q) = 0,\, \forall v_q \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G},\,\forall i>0.$}   		
	\end{proof}
	\iffalse	Consequently, \markbox{6240}{for} \markbox{6241}{the} \markbox{6242}{lift} \markbox{m6243}{$\tilde f:\mathbb S^m\times \mathbb{C}G_{n,k}\to \mathbb S^m\times \mathbb{C}G_{n,k}$}, \markbox{6244}{the} \markbox{6245}{induced} \markbox{6246}{maps} 
	\markbox{m6247}{$\tilde f^*:H^i_\times\to H^i_\times$} \markbox{6248}{and} \markbox{m6249}{$\tilde f_*:H_i^\times\to H_i^\times$} \markbox{6250}{are} \markbox{6251}{adjoint} \markbox{6252}{with} \markbox{6253}{respect} \markbox{6254}{to} \markbox{6255}{this} \markbox{6256}{perfect} \markbox{6257}{pairing,} \markbox{6258}{i.e.,}   
	\[
	\langle \tilde f^* \varphi, x\rangle=\langle \varphi, \tilde f_* x\rangle \text{ for all }\varphi\in H^i_{\times},x\in H_i^\times.
	\]\fi
	
	%To determine $\tilde f_*(U)$ when (iii) holds, write 
	%$\tilde f_*(U) = aU + \sum b_i v_i \in H_m^{\mathbb{S}} \oplus H_m^{\mathbb{C}G}\cong H_m^\times$.  
	%Then 
	%$\langle u, \tilde f_* U \rangle = \langle u, aU \rangle + \langle u, \sum b_i v_i \rangle = a + 0 = a$.  
	%On the other hand, 
	%$\langle u, \tilde f_* U \rangle = \langle \tilde f^* u, U \rangle = \langle \mu u, U \rangle = \mu$, 
	%so $a = \mu$.  
	%Proceeding similarly replacing  $u=\delta_U$  by $\delta_{v_i}$ yields $b_i = 0$ for all $i$.  
	%Hence, $\tilde f_*(U) = \mu U$.
	
	\iffalse	\markbox{6259}{\underline{When (i) and (iii) hold}}, \markbox{6260}{for} \markbox{6261}{any} \markbox{6262}{basis} \markbox{6263}{element} \markbox{m6264}{$v_q \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$}, \markbox{6265}{the} \markbox{6266}{coefficient} \markbox{6267}{of} \markbox{m6268}{$v_p$} \markbox{6269}{in} \markbox{m6270}{$\tilde f_*(v_q)$}, \markbox{6271}{,} \markbox{6272}{is} 
	\begin{equation}\label{i,ii,1}
		\langle \delta_{v_p}, \tilde f_*v_q\rangle
		= \langle \tilde f^* \delta_{v_p}, v_q\rangle
		= \langle \lambda^i \delta_{v_p}, v_q\rangle
		= \lambda^i \delta_{pq},
	\end{equation}
	\markbox{6273}{and} \markbox{6274}{the} \markbox{6275}{coefficient} \markbox{6276}{of} \markbox{m6277}{$\vartheta\otimes v_p \in \vartheta\otimes H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$} \markbox{6278}{in} \markbox{m6279}{$\tilde f_*(v_q)$} \markbox{6280}{is} 
	\begin{equation}\label{1,iii,2}
		\langle \delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p}, \tilde f_*v_q\rangle
		= \langle \tilde f^*(\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p}), v_q\rangle
		= \langle \mu\lambda^{i}\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p}, v_q\rangle
		= 0.
	\end{equation}
	\markbox{6281}{Thus,} \markbox{m6282}{$\tilde f_*(x) = \lambda^i x$}, \markbox{6283}{for} \markbox{6284}{all} \markbox{m6285}{$x \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$}. 
	\markbox{6286}{Also,} \markbox{6287}{the} \markbox{6288}{coefficient} \markbox{6289}{of} \markbox{m6290}{$v_p \in H_m^{\mathbb{C}G}$} \markbox{6291}{in} \markbox{m6292}{$\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q)$} \markbox{6293}{is} 
	\markbox{6294}{t} \markbox{6295}{of} \markbox{m6296}{$\vartheta\otimes v_p \in \vartheta \otimes H_{2i}^{{\mathbb CG}}$} \markbox{6297}{in} \markbox{m6298}{$\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q)$} \markbox{6299}{is} 
	\markbox{6300}{This} \markbox{6301}{shows} \markbox{6302}{that} \markbox{m6303}{$\tilde f_*(\vartheta \otimes x) = \mu \lambda^{i}\vartheta \otimes x$} \markbox{6304}{for} \markbox{6305}{all} \markbox{m6306}{$x\in \vartheta\otimes H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}$}.\fi
	
	\iffalse	\markbox{6307}{\underline{When (ii) and (iii) hold}},  \markbox{6308}{the} \markbox{6309}{coefficient} \markbox{6310}{of} \markbox{m6311}{$v_p$} (\markbox{m6312}{$p\neq 0$}) \markbox{6313}{in} \markbox{m6314}{$\tilde f_*(v_q)$}, \markbox{6315}{if} \markbox{m6316}{$\tilde f^*\delta_{v_p}=\sum a_i\delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_i} $},  is
	\[
	\langle \delta_{v_p}, \tilde f_*v_q\rangle=\langle\tilde f^*\delta_{v_p},v_q\rangle=\langle \sum a_i\delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_i},v_q\rangle=\sum 
	a_i\langle  \delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_i},v_q\rangle=0,
	\]
	\markbox{6317}{Thus,} \markbox{m6318}{$\tilde f_* (x)\in \vartheta\otimes H_*^{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{6319}{for} \markbox{6320}{all} \markbox{m6321}{$x\in H_*^{\mathbb CG}$}. \markbox{6322}{Also,} \markbox{6323}{the} \markbox{6324}{coefficient} \markbox{6325}{of} \markbox{m6326}{$\vartheta\otimes v_p$} \markbox{6327}{in} \markbox{m6328}{$\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q)$} is
	\[
	\langle \delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_p},\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q)\rangle=\langle\tilde f^*(\delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_p}), \vartheta \otimes v_q\rangle =
	\begin{cases}
		\langle \mu \delta_{\vartheta \otimes v_0}, \vartheta \otimes v_q\rangle=\mu\delta_{0q}& \text{if } p=0,\\
		\langle 0, \vartheta \otimes v_q\rangle =0& \text{if }p\neq 0.
	\end{cases}
	\]
	\markbox{6329}{Therefore,} \markbox{6330}{for} \markbox{6331}{all} \markbox{m6332}{$x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}$}, \markbox{m6333}{$\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes x)=\begin{cases}
		\mu \vartheta\otimes x +y \;\text{ for some }y\in H_{2i+m}^{\mathbb CG}  &\text{if } i=0 ,\\
		\quad \quad0 &\text{if }i>0.
	\end{cases}$} \fi
	
	\iffalse	\markbox{6334}{\underline{When (i) and (iv) hold}}, \markbox{6335}{the} \markbox{6336}{coefficient} \markbox{6337}{of} \markbox{m6338}{$v_p\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{6339}{in} \markbox{m6340}{$\tilde f_*(v_q)$} \markbox{6341}{is} 
	\[
	\langle \delta_{v_p},\tilde f_*(v_q)\rangle=\langle\tilde f^*\delta_{v_p},v_q\rangle=\langle \lambda^i\delta_{v_p},v_q\rangle=\lambda^i\delta_{pq}.
	\]
	\markbox{6342}{This} \markbox{6343}{implies} \markbox{6344}{that} \markbox{m6345}{$\tilde f_*(x)=\lambda^ix+\vartheta \otimes y$} \markbox{6346}{for} \markbox{6347}{some} \markbox{m6348}{$\vartheta \otimes y\in \vartheta \otimes H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}$}, \markbox{6349}{for} \markbox{6350}{all} \markbox{m6351}{$x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}$}. \fi
	
	
	\iffalse	\markbox{6352}{\underline{When (ii) and (iv) hold}}, \markbox{6353}{we} \markbox{6354}{can} \markbox{6355}{write} \markbox{m6356}{$\tilde f^*(\delta_{v_p})=\sum a_j\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_j}$} %and $\tilde f^*(\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_p})=\sum b_j\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_j}$
	for \markbox{6357}{some} \markbox{m6358}{$a_j\in \mathbb Q$} \markbox{6359}{and} \markbox{m6360}{$p\neq 0$}.
	\markbox{6361}{Now} \markbox{6362}{the} \markbox{6363}{coefficient} \markbox{6364}{of} \markbox{m6365}{$v_p$} \markbox{6366}{in} \markbox{m6367}{$\tilde f_*(v_q)$} is
	\[
	\langle \delta_{v_p},\tilde f_*v_q\rangle=\langle\tilde f^*\delta_{v_p}, v_q\rangle=\langle\sum a_j\delta_{\vartheta\otimes v_j}, v_q\rangle=0,
	\]
	\markbox{6368}{implying} \markbox{m6369}{$\tilde f_*(x)\in \vartheta\otimes H_*^{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{6370}{for} \markbox{6371}{all} \markbox{m6372}{$x\in H_*^{\mathbb CG}$}. \fi
	\iffalse
	Also, \markbox{6373}{the} \markbox{6374}{coefficient} \markbox{6375}{of} \markbox{m6376}{$ v_p$} \markbox{6377}{in} \markbox{m6378}{$\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q)$} is
	\[
	\langle \delta_{v_p},\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes v_q)\rangle=\langle\tilde f^*\delta_{v_p}, \vartheta\otimes v_q\rangle=\langle\sum b_j\delta_{v_j},\vartheta\otimes v_q\rangle=0.
	\]
	\markbox{6379}{This} \markbox{6380}{ensures} \markbox{6381}{that} \markbox{m6382}{$\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes x)\in H_*^{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{6383}{for} \markbox{6384}{all} \markbox{m6385}{$\vartheta\otimes x\in \vartheta\otimes H_*^{\mathbb CG}$}.
	
	
	\markbox{6386}{We} \markbox{6387}{refer} \markbox{6388}{to} \markbox{6389}{the} \markbox{6390}{above} \markbox{6391}{observations} \markbox{6392}{from} \markbox{6393}{any} \markbox{6394}{combination} \markbox{6395}{of} \markbox{6396}{one} \markbox{6397}{condition} \markbox{6398}{from} 
	\markbox{m6399}{$(\mathrm{i}),(\mathrm{ii})$} \markbox{6400}{and} \markbox{6401}{one} \markbox{6402}{from} \markbox{m6403}{$(\mathrm{iii}),(\mathrm{iv})$}, \markbox{6404}{by} \markbox{6405}{the} \markbox{6406}{symbol} \markbox{m6407}{$\mathscr{X}$}.
	
	
	
	%Summarizing above, we have for all $x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}$,
	%\[
	%\tilde f_*(x)=
	%\begin{cases}
	%   \lambda^ix  &\text{ if (i) and (iii) hold},\\
	%    \lambda^ix +\vartheta\otimes y, \text{ for some }y\in H_*^{\mathbb CG}& \text{ if (i) and (iv) hold}.
	%^\end{cases}
%\]


\vspace{.2in}\fi

\iffalse
******

Thus, \markbox{6408}{for} \markbox{6409}{all} \markbox{m6410}{$x \in H^{\mathbb CG}_{2i}$}, \markbox{m6411}{$\varphi \in H^{2i}_{\mathbb CG}$}, \markbox{6412}{and} \markbox{m6413}{$y \in H^m_\times$}, \markbox{6414}{we} have
\begin{equation}\label{}
	\langle \varphi, \tilde f_* x\rangle =
	\begin{cases}
		\langle \varphi, \lambda_1^i x\rangle & \text{if (i) holds,} \\
		\langle u P_{\varphi}, x\rangle & \text{if (ii) holds},\\
	\end{cases}
	\quad \text{and} \quad
	\langle u, \tilde f_* y\rangle =
	\begin{cases}
		\langle u, \mu_1 y\rangle & \text{if (iii) holds,} \\
		& \text{if (iv) holds}.\\
	\end{cases}
\end{equation}

Therefore, \markbox{6415}{for} \markbox{6416}{all} \markbox{m6417}{$x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb CG}$}, \markbox{m6418}{$\tilde f_*(x)=\lambda_1^ix$} \markbox{6419}{if} \markbox{6420}{(i)} \markbox{6421}{holds,} \markbox{m6422}{$\tilde f_*(x)\in [\mathbb S^m]\otimes H_{2i-m}^{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{6423}{if} \markbox{6424}{(ii)} \markbox{6425}{holds,} \markbox{6426}{and} \markbox{m6427}{$\tilde f_*([\mathbb S^m])=\mu_1 [\mathbb S^m]$} \markbox{6428}{if} \markbox{6429}{(iii)} \markbox{6430}{holds,} \markbox{6431}{where} \markbox{m6432}{$[\mathbb S^m]\in H_m^{\mathbb S}$} \markbox{6433}{denotes} \markbox{6434}{the} \markbox{6435}{fundamental} \markbox{6436}{class} \markbox{6437}{of} \markbox{m6438}{$\mathbb S^m$} \markbox{6439}{satisfying} \markbox{m6440}{$\langle u,[\mathbb S^m]\rangle=1.$}
\fi


\subsection{} \markbox{6441}{The} \markbox{6442}{following} \markbox{6443}{theorems} \markbox{6444}{provide} \markbox{6445}{a} \markbox{6446}{criteria} \markbox{6447}{for} \markbox{6448}{the} \markbox{6449}{existence} \markbox{6450}{of} \markbox{6451}{coincidence} \markbox{6452}{points} \markbox{6453}{between} \markbox{6454}{a} \markbox{6455}{pair} \markbox{6456}{of} \markbox{6457}{continuous} \markbox{6458}{functions} \markbox{6459}{on} \markbox{m6460}{$P(m,n,k)$}.

\begin{theorem}\label{coincidence thm}
	\markbox{6461}{Let} \markbox{m6462}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{6463}{be} \markbox{6464}{a} \markbox{6465}{generalized} \markbox{6466}{Dold} \markbox{6467}{manifold} \markbox{6468}{with} \markbox{m6469}{$k<n-k$} \markbox{6470}{and} \markbox{m6471}{$k(n-k)$} \markbox{6472}{even.} \markbox{6473}{Let} \markbox{m6474}{$f$} \markbox{6475}{and} \markbox{m6476}{$g$} \markbox{6477}{be} \markbox{6478}{two} \markbox{6479}{continuous} \markbox{6480}{maps} \markbox{6481}{on} \markbox{m6482}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{6483}{and} \markbox{m6484}{$\tilde f, \tilde g$} \markbox{6485}{be} \markbox{6486}{their} \markbox{6487}{lifts} \markbox{6488}{as} \markbox{6489}{defined} \markbox{6490}{in}  \markbox{6491}{Remark} \ref{lift} \markbox{6492}{such} that
	%and suppose that the induced endomorphisms in cohomology satisfies:	
	\begin{enumerate}	
		\item {} \markbox{m6493}{$g^*$} \markbox{6494}{is} \markbox{6495}{an} \markbox{6496}{automorphism} \markbox{6497}{of} \markbox{m6498}{$H^*(P(m,n,k);\mathbb Q)$}. 
		\item {} \markbox{m6499}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_1) \neq au,\, a \in \mathbb{Q}$}.
		\item {} \markbox{m6500}{$\deg(p\circ g \circ s)\neq -\deg (p\circ f\circ s)$} \markbox{6501}{if} \markbox{m6502}{$m$} \markbox{6503}{is} odd.
	\end{enumerate}
	\markbox{6504}{where} \markbox{m6505}{$s$} \markbox{6506}{denotes} \markbox{6507}{a} \markbox{6508}{section} \markbox{6509}{of} \markbox{6510}{the} \markbox{m6511}{$X$}-bundle \markbox{6512}{projection} \markbox{m6513}{$p$} \markbox{6514}{defined} \markbox{6515}{in} \eqref{sectio} \markbox{6516}{and} \eqref{proj}.	\markbox{6517}{Then,} \markbox{6518}{there} \markbox{6519}{is} \markbox{6520}{a} \markbox{6521}{point} \markbox{6522}{of} \markbox{6523}{coincidence} \markbox{6524}{of} \markbox{m6525}{$f$} \markbox{6526}{and}  \markbox{m6527}{$g$}.
\end{theorem}
\begin{proof}
	\markbox{6528}{Using} \corref{automor}, \markbox{6529}{we} \markbox{6530}{have} \markbox{m6531}{$\tilde g^*$} \markbox{6532}{is} \markbox{6533}{an} \markbox{6534}{automorphism} \markbox{6535}{on} \markbox{m6536}{$H^*_{\times}$} \markbox{6537}{given} by
	\markbox{m6538}{$\tilde g^*(c_i) = \lambda_1^i c_i$}, \markbox{6539}{and} \markbox{m6540}{$\tilde g^*(u) = \mu_1 u$} \markbox{6541}{for} \markbox{6542}{some} \markbox{m6543}{$\lambda_1, \mu_1 \in \mathbb{Q}\backslash \{0\}$} \markbox{6544}{if} \markbox{m6545}{$k<n-k$}.
	
	\markbox{6546}{Using} \lemref{image of homf}, \markbox{6547}{there} \markbox{6548}{exist} \markbox{m6549}{$\lambda \in \mathbb{Q}\backslash \{0\}$} \markbox{6550}{and} \markbox{m6551}{$\mu \in \mathbb{Q}$} \markbox{6552}{such} \markbox{6553}{that} \markbox{m6554}{$\tilde{f}_*$} \markbox{6555}{is} \markbox{6556}{of} \markbox{6557}{the} \markbox{6558}{following} \markbox{6559}{form,} 
	\begin{equation}\label{flower star}
		\begin{split}
			\tilde f_*(x)=\lambda^ix+\vartheta\otimes y, \text{ for some }y\in H_{2i-m}^{\mathbb CG}, \, \forall x \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}\\
			\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes x)=\mu\lambda^i (\vartheta\otimes x) , \text{ or } \tilde{f}_*(\vartheta \otimes x) = z, \text{ for some }z\in H_{2i+m}^{\mathbb CG},\, \forall x \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}
		\end{split}
	\end{equation}
	\markbox{6560}{To} \markbox{6561}{prove} \markbox{6562}{that} \markbox{m6563}{$f$} \markbox{6564}{has} \markbox{6565}{a} \markbox{6566}{point} \markbox{6567}{of} \markbox{6568}{coincidence} \markbox{6569}{with} \markbox{m6570}{$g$}, \markbox{6571}{it} \markbox{6572}{is} \markbox{6573}{sufficient} \markbox{6574}{to} \markbox{6575}{prove} \markbox{6576}{that} \markbox{6577}{either} \markbox{m6578}{$\tilde{f}$} \markbox{6579}{or} \markbox{6580}{the} \markbox{6581}{composition} \markbox{m6582}{$\theta \circ \tilde{f} $} \markbox{6583}{has} \markbox{6584}{a} \markbox{6585}{point} \markbox{6586}{of} \markbox{6587}{coincidence} \markbox{6588}{with} \markbox{m6589}{$g$} \markbox{6590}{where} \markbox{m6591}{$\theta = \alpha \times \sigma$} \markbox{6592}{defined} \markbox{6593}{in} \secref{gds}. \markbox{6594}{By} \thmref{LCT}, \markbox{6595}{we} \markbox{6596}{need} \markbox{6597}{to} \markbox{6598}{compute} \markbox{m6599}{$L(\tilde f, \tilde g)$} \markbox{6600}{and} \markbox{m6601}{$L(\theta \circ \tilde f, \tilde g)$}.
	
	\markbox{6602}{For} \markbox{m6603}{$x\in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}$}, \markbox{6604}{we} \markbox{6605}{have} 
	\begin{equation*}\label{D cal}
		\begin{split}
			D\tilde g^* D^{-1} \tilde f_*(x)=\mu_1 \lambda^i\lambda_1^{d-i} x + \vartheta\otimes y'\text{ for some }y' \in H^{\mathbb CG}_{2i-m}\\
			D\tilde g^* D^{-1} \tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes x)= \mu \lambda^i\lambda_1^{d-i}(\vartheta\otimes x)+z' \text{ for some }z'\in H_{2i+m}^{\mathbb CG}.
		\end{split}
	\end{equation*}
	\markbox{6606}{where} \markbox{m6607}{$z^{'} =0$} \markbox{6608}{or} \markbox{m6609}{$\mu =0$} \markbox{6610}{depending} \markbox{6611}{on} \markbox{6612}{the} \markbox{6613}{image} \markbox{6614}{of} \markbox{m6615}{$\tilde{f}_*(\vartheta \otimes x)$}.
	%Now we compute the Lefschetz number of the map $L(\tilde{f},\tilde g)$  and $L(\theta\circ \tilde f, \tilde g)$ under the consideration that $\lambda=0$ if (ii) holds and $\mu=0$ if (iv) holds. 
	Recall \markbox{6616}{that}  \markbox{m6617}{$d_{2i}$} \markbox{6618}{denote} \markbox{6619}{the} \markbox{6620}{dimension} \markbox{m6621}{$\dim H^{2i}_{\mathbb CG}$}. \markbox{6622}{The} \markbox{6623}{Lefschetz} \markbox{6624}{number}  \markbox{m6625}{$L(\tilde{f},\tilde g)$} is
	\begin{equation*}\label{L(f,g)}
		L(\tilde f,\tilde g) =(\mu_1 + \mu) \sum_{i=0}^{k(n-k)} d_{2i} \lambda^i\lambda_1^{d-i}.
	\end{equation*}
	\markbox{6626}{Using} \markbox{6627}{the} \lemref{sum neq 0} \markbox{6628}{and} \markbox{6629}{the} \markbox{6630}{fact} \markbox{6631}{that} \markbox{m6632}{$\lambda_1\neq 0$}, \markbox{6633}{the} sum
	\[
	\sum_{i=0}^{k(n-k)} d_{2i} \lambda^i\lambda_1^{d-i}=\lambda_1^d\sum_{i=0}^{k(n-k)} d_{2i} (\lambda/\lambda_1)^i\neq 0,
	\]
	\markbox{6634}{Since} \markbox{m6635}{$\tilde f\circ\theta=\theta\circ \tilde f$}, \markbox{6636}{it} \markbox{6637}{follows} \markbox{6638}{that} $$(\theta\circ \tilde  f )^*(c_i)= (-1)^i \tilde{f}^*(c_i), \forall i \in I, \quad (\theta \circ\tilde  f)^*(u)=\begin{cases}
		-\tilde  f^*(u), \text{ if } m \text{ is even,}\\
		\tilde  f^*(u), \text{ if } m \text{ is odd}.
	\end{cases}$$ 
%	If $m$ is odd, using $\deg(p\circ g \circ s)\neq -\deg (p\circ f\circ s)$ i.e. $\mu_1 \neq -\mu$, we have $L(\theta\circ\tilde f, \tilde g) = L(\tilde f, \tilde g)\neq 0$ and we have the result. \\
	If \markbox{m6639}{$m$} \markbox{6640}{is} \markbox{6641}{even,} \markbox{6642}{then}  
	\begin{equation*}\label{D with theta}
		\begin{split}
			D\tilde g^* D^{-1} (\theta\circ \tilde f)_*(x)=\mu_1(- \lambda)^i\lambda_1^{d-i} x + \vartheta\otimes y''\text{ for some }y'' \in H^{\mathbb CG}_{2i-m} \\
			D\tilde g^* D^{-1} (\theta\circ \tilde f)_*(\vartheta\otimes x)= -\mu (-\lambda)^i\lambda_1^{d-i}\vartheta\otimes x+z'' \text{ for some }z''\in H_{2i+m}^{\mathbb CG}.
		\end{split}
	\end{equation*}
	\markbox{6643}{Thus,}  \markbox{6644}{the} \markbox{6645}{Lefschetz} \markbox{6646}{number} is
	\begin{equation*}\label{L(theta f,g)}
		L(\theta \circ\tilde f,\tilde g) =(\mu_1 - \mu)\sum_{i=0}^{k(n-k)} d_{2i} (-\lambda)^i\lambda_1^{d-i}.
	\end{equation*}
	\markbox{6647}{Also,} \markbox{6648}{using}  \markbox{m6649}{$\mu_1\neq 0$} \markbox{6650}{and} \lemref{sum neq 0}  \markbox{6651}{it} \markbox{6652}{follows} \markbox{6653}{that} \markbox{6654}{that} \markbox{6655}{either} \markbox{m6656}{$L(\tilde f, \tilde g)$} \markbox{6657}{or} \markbox{m6658}{$L(\theta\circ \tilde f,\tilde g)$} \markbox{6659}{is} \markbox{6660}{nonzero.} 
	
	\markbox{6661}{If} \markbox{m6662}{$m$} \markbox{6663}{is} \markbox{6664}{odd,} \markbox{m6665}{$	L(\theta \circ\tilde f,\tilde g) =(\mu_1 + \mu)\sum_{i=0}^{k(n-k)} d_{2i} (-\lambda)^i\lambda_1^{d-i}.$} \markbox{6666}{Using}  \lemref{sum neq 0} \markbox{6667}{and} \markbox{m6668}{$\deg(p\circ g \circ s)\neq -\deg (p\circ f\circ s)$} \markbox{6669}{that} \markbox{6670}{is} \markbox{m6671}{$\mu_1 \neq -\mu$}, \markbox{6672}{we} \markbox{6673}{have} \markbox{6674}{both} \markbox{m6675}{$L(\tilde{f},\tilde{g})$} \markbox{6676}{and} \markbox{m6677}{$L(\theta \circ\tilde f,\tilde g)$} \markbox{6678}{are} \markbox{6679}{nonzero.} 
	\markbox{6680}{This} \markbox{6681}{ensures} \markbox{6682}{that} \markbox{6683}{there} \markbox{6684}{exist} \markbox{6685}{a} \markbox{6686}{point} \markbox{6687}{of} \markbox{6688}{conincidence} \markbox{6689}{between} \markbox{m6690}{$f $} \markbox{6691}{and} \markbox{m6692}{$g$}.
\end{proof}
%	Using  \remref{lemrem} in the case $k=n-k$, we need to replace $\lambda$ by $-\lambda$ in \eqref{flower star} if $\tilde{f}^*(c_i) = -\lambda^i c_i$. In the rest of the calculations, $\lambda$ will be replaced by $-\lambda$ and we get the same result.
\begin{theorem}\label{coincidence thm under hom}
	\markbox{6693}{Let} \markbox{m6694}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{6695}{be} \markbox{6696}{a} \markbox{6697}{generalized} \markbox{6698}{Dold} \markbox{6699}{manifold} \markbox{6700}{with} \markbox{m6701}{$k(n-k)$} \markbox{6702}{even} \markbox{6703}{and} \markbox{6704}{assume} \markbox{6705}{that} \markbox{6706}{the} \markbox{6707}{hypothesis} \eqref{Homer} \markbox{6708}{is} \markbox{6709}{satisfied.} \markbox{6710}{Let} \markbox{m6711}{$g$} \markbox{6712}{and} \markbox{m6713}{$f$} \markbox{6714}{are} \markbox{6715}{two} \markbox{6716}{continuous} \markbox{6717}{maps} \markbox{6718}{on} \markbox{m6719}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{6720}{and} \markbox{m6721}{$\tilde g, \tilde f$} \markbox{6722}{be} \markbox{6723}{their} \markbox{6724}{lifts} \markbox{6725}{as} \markbox{6726}{defined} \markbox{6727}{in}  \markbox{6728}{Remark} \ref{lift} \markbox{6729}{such} that
	%and suppose that the induced endomorphisms in cohomology satisfies:	
	\begin{enumerate}	
		\item {} \markbox{m6730}{$g^*$} \markbox{6731}{is} \markbox{6732}{an} \markbox{6733}{automorphism} \markbox{6734}{of} \markbox{m6735}{$H^*(P(m,n,k);\mathbb Q)$}. 
		\item {} \markbox{m6736}{$\tilde{f}^*(u) = \mu u,\, \mu \in \mathbb{Q}$} \markbox{6737}{if} \markbox{m6738}{$\tilde{f}^*(H^*_{\mathbb CG}) \nsubseteq H^*_{\mathbb CG}$} \markbox{6739}{and} \markbox{m6740}{$m$} \markbox{6741}{is} even.
		\item {} \markbox{m6742}{$\deg(p\circ g \circ s)\neq -\deg (p\circ f\circ s)$} \markbox{6743}{if} \markbox{m6744}{$m$} \markbox{6745}{is} odd.
	\end{enumerate}
	\markbox{m6746}{$s$} \markbox{6747}{denotes} \markbox{6748}{a} \markbox{6749}{section} \markbox{6750}{of} \markbox{6751}{the} \markbox{m6752}{$X$}-bundle \markbox{6753}{projection} \markbox{m6754}{$p$} \markbox{6755}{defined} \markbox{6756}{in} \eqref{sectio} \markbox{6757}{and} \eqref{proj}. \markbox{6758}{Then,} \markbox{6759}{there} \markbox{6760}{is} \markbox{6761}{a} \markbox{6762}{point} \markbox{6763}{of} \markbox{6764}{coincidence} \markbox{6765}{of} \markbox{m6766}{$f$} \markbox{6767}{and}  \markbox{m6768}{$g$}.
\end{theorem}
\begin{proof}
	\markbox{6769}{If} \markbox{m6770}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_1) \neq au, \, a\in \mathbb{Q}$} \markbox{6771}{then} \markbox{6772}{we} \markbox{6773}{have} \markbox{6774}{the} \markbox{6775}{result} \markbox{6776}{by} \thmref{coincidence thm}.\\ \markbox{6777}{Let} \markbox{6778}{us} \markbox{6779}{consider} \markbox{6780}{the} \markbox{6781}{other} \markbox{6782}{case} \markbox{6783}{when} \markbox{m6784}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_1) = au, \, a\in \mathbb{Q}$}, \markbox{6785}{using} \thmref{main thm 2} \markbox{6786}{we} \markbox{6787}{have} \markbox{m6788}{$\tilde{f}^*(c_i) = uP_i, \text{ for some } P_i\in H^{2i-m}_{\mathbb{C}G}.$} 
	
	\markbox{6789}{If} \markbox{m6790}{$P_i \neq 0$} \markbox{6791}{for} \markbox{6792}{some} \markbox{m6793}{$i$} \markbox{6794}{in} \markbox{m6795}{$I$} \markbox{6796}{then} \markbox{m6797}{$\tilde{f}^*(H^*_{\mathbb CG}) \nsubseteq H^*_{\mathbb CG}$}. \markbox{6798}{Since} \markbox{m6799}{$\tilde{f}^*$} \markbox{6800}{is} \markbox{6801}{graded} \markbox{6802}{and} \markbox{6803}{by} \markbox{6804}{\textit{(2)}} \markbox{6805}{we} \markbox{6806}{have} \markbox{m6807}{$\tilde{f}^*(u) = \mu u,\, \mu \in \mathbb{Q}$}. \markbox{6808}{Using} \lemref{image of homf under hom}, \markbox{m6809}{$\tilde{f}_*$} \markbox{6810}{is} \markbox{6811}{of} \markbox{6812}{the} \markbox{6813}{following} \markbox{6814}{form,} \begin{equation}\label{uin CG}
		\begin{split}
			\tilde f_*(x)= \vartheta\otimes y, \text{ for some }y\in H_{2i-m}^{\mathbb CG}, \, \forall x \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}, \, i>0\\
			\tilde f_*(\vartheta\otimes x)=\mu(\vartheta\otimes x) +z, \text{ for some }z\in H_{2i+m}^{\mathbb CG},\, \forall x \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}
		\end{split}
	\end{equation}
	\markbox{6815}{where} \markbox{m6816}{$\mu =0$} \markbox{6817}{if} \markbox{m6818}{$i>0$}. \markbox{6819}{By} \corref{automor}, \markbox{6820}{we} \markbox{6821}{have} \markbox{m6822}{$\tilde g^*$} \markbox{6823}{is} \markbox{6824}{an} \markbox{6825}{automorphism} \markbox{6826}{on} \markbox{m6827}{$H^*_{\times}$} \markbox{6828}{given} by
	\markbox{m6829}{$\tilde g^*(c_i) = \lambda_1^i c_i$}, \markbox{6830}{and} \markbox{m6831}{$\tilde g^*(u) = \mu_1 u$} \markbox{6832}{for} \markbox{6833}{some} \markbox{m6834}{$\lambda_1, \mu_1 \in \mathbb{Q}\backslash \{0\}$}. \markbox{6835}{Using} \thmref{LCT} \markbox{6836}{and} \markbox{6837}{the} \markbox{6838}{similar} \markbox{6839}{calculations} \markbox{6840}{as} \markbox{6841}{done} \markbox{6842}{in} \markbox{6843}{the} \markbox{6844}{proof} \markbox{6845}{of} \thmref{coincidence thm}, \markbox{6846}{we} \markbox{6847}{get} $$L(\tilde f,\tilde g) =(\mu_1 + \mu) d_0 \lambda_1^d, \quad L(\theta \circ\tilde f,\tilde g) =\begin{cases}
		(\mu_1 - \mu)d_{0} \lambda_1^{d},  \text{ if } m \text{ is even,}\\
		(\mu_1 +\mu)d_{0} \lambda_1^{d},  \text{ if } m \text{ is odd.}
	\end{cases}$$ \markbox{6848}{Using} \markbox{m6849}{$\lambda_1 \neq 0$} \markbox{6850}{and} \markbox{m6851}{$\mu_1 \neq 0$}, \markbox{6852}{either} \markbox{m6853}{$L(\tilde f,\tilde g) $} \markbox{6854}{or} \markbox{m6855}{$ L(\theta \circ\tilde f,\tilde g)$} \markbox{6856}{is} \markbox{6857}{non} \markbox{6858}{zero} \markbox{6859}{if} \markbox{m6860}{$m$} \markbox{6861}{is} \markbox{6862}{even.} \markbox{6863}{Using} \markbox{m6864}{$\deg(p\circ g \circ s)\neq -\deg (p\circ f\circ s)$} \markbox{6865}{i.e.} \markbox{m6866}{$\mu_1 \neq -\mu$} \markbox{6867}{we} \markbox{6868}{have} \markbox{m6869}{$L(\tilde f, \tilde g) = L(\theta \circ \tilde f, \tilde g) \neq 0$}.  \markbox{6870}{Hence,} \markbox{6871}{we} \markbox{6872}{get} \markbox{6873}{the} result.
	
	\markbox{6874}{Let} \markbox{6875}{us} \markbox{6876}{consider} \markbox{6877}{the} \markbox{6878}{case} \markbox{6879}{when} \markbox{m6880}{$P_i =0,\, \forall i \in I$}, \markbox{6881}{if} \markbox{m6882}{$\tilde{f}^*(u) = \mu u, \mu \in \mathbb{Q}$} \markbox{6883}{then} \markbox{6884}{the} \markbox{6885}{proof} \markbox{6886}{remains} \markbox{6887}{exactly} \markbox{6888}{the} \markbox{6889}{same} \markbox{6890}{as} \markbox{6891}{given} \markbox{6892}{above.} \markbox{6893}{We} \markbox{6894}{need} \markbox{6895}{to} \markbox{6896}{focus} \markbox{6897}{on} \markbox{6898}{the} \markbox{6899}{case} \markbox{6900}{when} \markbox{m6901}{$\tilde{f}^*(u)\in H^*_{\mathbb{C}G}$}. \markbox{6902}{Using} \lemref{image of homf under hom} \markbox{6903}{and} \eqref{computation}, \markbox{6904}{we} \markbox{6905}{have} $$\tilde{f}_*(x) = \vartheta \otimes y, \text{ for some }y\in H_{2i-m}^{\mathbb CG}, \, \forall x \in H_{2i}^{\mathbb{C}G}, \, i>0, \quad \tilde{f}_*(\vartheta \otimes x) \in H_*^{\mathbb{C}G}, \forall x\in  H_*^{\mathbb{C}G}.$$ \markbox{6906}{This} \markbox{6907}{is} \markbox{6908}{exactly} \markbox{6909}{the} \markbox{6910}{same} \markbox{6911}{if} \markbox{6912}{we} \markbox{6913}{take} \markbox{m6914}{$\mu =0$} \markbox{6915}{in} \eqref{uin CG}. \markbox{6916}{The} \markbox{6917}{rest} \markbox{6918}{of} \markbox{6919}{the} \markbox{6920}{calculations} \markbox{6921}{also} \markbox{6922}{remains} \markbox{6923}{the} \markbox{6924}{same} \markbox{6925}{and} \markbox{6926}{we} \markbox{6927}{get} \markbox{6928}{the} result.
\end{proof}



\begin{remark}
	\markbox{6929}{There} \markbox{6930}{are} \markbox{6931}{many} \markbox{6932}{situations} \markbox{6933}{when} \markbox{6934}{the} \markbox{6935}{map} \markbox{m6936}{$f$} \markbox{6937}{satisfies} \markbox{6938}{the} \markbox{6939}{required} \markbox{6940}{hypothesis} \markbox{6941}{\textit{(2)}} \markbox{6942}{considered} \markbox{6943}{in} \thmref{coincidence thm} \markbox{6944}{or} \thmref{coincidence thm under hom}. \markbox{6945}{Some} \markbox{6946}{of} \markbox{6947}{them} \markbox{6948}{are} \markbox{6949}{as} \markbox{6950}{follows:} 
	\begin{enumerate}
		\item {} The \markbox{6951}{lift} \markbox{m6952}{$\tilde f$} \markbox{6953}{stabilizes} \markbox{6954}{a} \markbox{6955}{copy} \markbox{6956}{of} \markbox{6957}{Grassmannian,} \markbox{6958}{i.e.,} \markbox{m6959}{$\tilde f(\{x_0\}\times\mathbb CG_{n,k})\subseteq \{x_0\}\times\mathbb CG_{n,k}$} \markbox{6960}{for} \markbox{6961}{some} \markbox{m6962}{$x_0\in \mathbb S^m$}. 
		\item  {} The \markbox{6963}{map} \markbox{m6964}{$p_1\circ \tilde f^*\circ i_1: H^*_{\mathbb CG}\to H^*_{\mathbb C G}$} \markbox{6965}{is} \markbox{6966}{an} \markbox{6967}{automorphism,} \markbox{6968}{equivalently,} \markbox{m6969}{$f^*(c_1^2)=\lambda^2c_1^2,\, \lambda\in \mathbb Q\backslash \{0\},$} \markbox{6970}{where} \markbox{m6971}{$p_1$} \markbox{6972}{and} \markbox{m6973}{$i_1$} \markbox{6974}{are} \markbox{6975}{defined} \markbox{6976}{in} \eqref{comm diagram}.
		\item {} The \markbox{6977}{map} \markbox{m6978}{$p_2\circ \tilde f\circ i_1:\mathbb S^m\to \mathbb CG_{n,k}$} \markbox{6979}{is} \markbox{6980}{rationally} \markbox{6981}{null} \markbox{6982}{homotopic,} \markbox{6983}{where} \markbox{m6984}{$p_2$} \markbox{6985}{is} \markbox{6986}{the} \markbox{6987}{projection} \markbox{6988}{onto} \markbox{6989}{the} \markbox{6990}{second} \markbox{6991}{summand} \markbox{6992}{and} \markbox{m6993}{$i_1$} \markbox{6994}{is} \markbox{6995}{the} \markbox{6996}{inclusion} \markbox{6997}{into} \markbox{6998}{the} \markbox{6999}{first} \markbox{7000}{summand.} %$i_1:\mathbb S^m\hookrightarrow\mathbb S^m\times \mathbb CG_{n,k}$ be the inclusion into the first component and $p_2:\mathbb S^m\times \mathbb CG_{n,k}\to \mathbb CG_{n,k}$ be the projection onto the second component.
	\end{enumerate} 
\end{remark}



	\markbox{7001}{Under} \markbox{7002}{the} \markbox{7003}{assumption} \markbox{m7004}{$m>2k$}, \markbox{7005}{any} \markbox{7006}{continuous} \markbox{7007}{map} \markbox{m7008}{$f$} \markbox{7009}{on} \markbox{7010}{the} \markbox{7011}{generalized} \markbox{7012}{Dold} \markbox{7013}{space} \markbox{m7014}{$P(m,n,k)$}, \markbox{7015}{the} \markbox{7016}{lift} \markbox{m7017}{$\tilde f$} \markbox{7018}{(from} Remark~\ref{lift}) \markbox{7019}{satisfies} \markbox{m7020}{$\tilde f^{*}(c_i)=\lambda^ic_i$} \markbox{7021}{for} \markbox{7022}{all} \markbox{m7023}{$i\in I$}. \markbox{7024}{Hence} condition~\markbox{7025}{\textit{(2)}} \markbox{7026}{of} Theorem~\ref{coincidence thm under hom} \markbox{7027}{may} \markbox{7028}{be} \markbox{7029}{omitted,} \markbox{7030}{and} \markbox{7031}{one} \markbox{7032}{obtains} \markbox{7033}{the} \markbox{7034}{following} consequence.
	\begin{corollary}
		\markbox{7035}{Let} \markbox{m7036}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{7037}{be} \markbox{7038}{a} \markbox{7039}{generalized} \markbox{7040}{Dold} \markbox{7041}{space} \markbox{7042}{with} \markbox{m7043}{$m$} \markbox{7044}{and} \markbox{m7045}{$k(n-k)$} \markbox{7046}{both} \markbox{7047}{even.} \markbox{7048}{Assume} \markbox{m7049}{$m>2k$}, \markbox{7050}{and} \markbox{7051}{the} \markbox{7052}{hypothesis} \eqref{Homer} \markbox{7053}{is} satisfied.
		\markbox{7054}{Then,} \markbox{7055}{for} \markbox{7056}{any} \markbox{7057}{continuous} \markbox{7058}{function} \markbox{m7059}{$g$} \markbox{7060}{on} \markbox{m7061}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{7062}{that} \markbox{7063}{induces} \markbox{7064}{an} \markbox{7065}{automorphism} \markbox{7066}{on} \markbox{m7067}{$H^*(P(m,n,k);\mathbb{Q})$}, \markbox{7068}{the} \markbox{7069}{pair} \markbox{m7070}{$(P(m,n,k),g)$} \markbox{7071}{has} \markbox{7072}{the} \markbox{7073}{coincidence} \markbox{7074}{property.} \\ \markbox{7075}{In} \markbox{7076}{particular,} \markbox{7077}{for} \markbox{m7078}{$g=\mathrm{id}$}, \markbox{7079}{the} \markbox{7080}{space} \markbox{m7081}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{7082}{has} \markbox{7083}{the} \markbox{7084}{fixed-point} property.
	\end{corollary}










In \thmref{coincidence thm under hom}, \markbox{7085}{the} \markbox{7086}{first} \markbox{7087}{assumption} \markbox{7088}{that} \markbox{m7089}{$g^*$} \markbox{7090}{is} \markbox{7091}{an} \markbox{7092}{automorphism} \markbox{7093}{of} \markbox{m7094}{$H^*(P(m,n,k); \mathbb{Q})$} \markbox{7095}{can} \markbox{7096}{be} \markbox{7097}{relaxed} \markbox{7098}{by} \markbox{7099}{assuming} \markbox{m7100}{$\mu$} \markbox{7101}{is} \markbox{7102}{nonzero,} \markbox{7103}{which} \markbox{7104}{leads} \markbox{7105}{to} \markbox{7106}{the} \markbox{7107}{following} \markbox{7108}{proposition.} 
\begin{proposition}
	\markbox{7109}{Let} \markbox{m7110}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{7111}{be} \markbox{7112}{a} \markbox{7113}{generalized} \markbox{7114}{Dold} \markbox{7115}{manifold} \markbox{7116}{with} \markbox{m7117}{$k(n-k)$} \markbox{7118}{even} \markbox{7119}{and} \markbox{7120}{assume} \markbox{7121}{that} \markbox{7122}{the} \markbox{7123}{hypothesis} \eqref{Homer} \markbox{7124}{is} \markbox{7125}{satisfied.} \markbox{7126}{Let} \markbox{m7127}{$g$} \markbox{7128}{and} \markbox{m7129}{$f$} \markbox{7130}{are} \markbox{7131}{two} \markbox{7132}{continuous} \markbox{7133}{maps} \markbox{7134}{on} \markbox{m7135}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{7136}{and} \markbox{m7137}{$\tilde g, \tilde f$} \markbox{7138}{be} \markbox{7139}{their} \markbox{7140}{lifts} \markbox{7141}{as} \markbox{7142}{defined} \markbox{7143}{in}  \markbox{7144}{Remark} \ref{lift} \markbox{7145}{such} that
	\begin{enumerate}
		\item {} \markbox{m7146}{$\tilde g^*(H^*_{\mathbb CG})= H^*_{\mathbb CG}$}.
		\item {} \markbox{m7147}{$\tilde f^*(u)=\mu u,\, \mu\in \mathbb Q\backslash \{0\}$}
	\end{enumerate}
Then, \markbox{7148}{there} \markbox{7149}{is} \markbox{7150}{a} \markbox{7151}{point} \markbox{7152}{of} \markbox{7153}{coincidence} \markbox{7154}{of} \markbox{m7155}{$f$} \markbox{7156}{and}  \markbox{m7157}{$g$}.
\end{proposition}
The \markbox{7158}{proof} \markbox{7159}{of} \markbox{7160}{the} \markbox{7161}{above} \markbox{7162}{proposition} \markbox{7163}{is} \markbox{7164}{similar} \markbox{7165}{to} \markbox{7166}{the} \markbox{7167}{proof} \markbox{7168}{of} \thmref{coincidence thm under hom}. \markbox{7169}{Therefore,} \markbox{7170}{we} \markbox{7171}{omit} \markbox{7172}{the} details.

\iffalse \begin{proposition}
	\markbox{7173}{Let} \markbox{m7174}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{7175}{be} \markbox{7176}{a} \markbox{7177}{generalized} \markbox{7178}{Dold} \markbox{7179}{manifold.} \markbox{7180}{Consider} \markbox{7181}{two} \markbox{7182}{continuous} \markbox{7183}{maps} \markbox{m7184}{$f,g$} \markbox{7185}{on} \markbox{m7186}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{7187}{and} \markbox{m7188}{$\tilde f, \tilde g$} \markbox{7189}{be} \markbox{7190}{their} \markbox{7191}{lifts} \markbox{7192}{as} \markbox{7193}{defined} \markbox{7194}{in}  \markbox{7195}{Remark} \ref{lift}.
	\markbox{7196}{Suppose} \markbox{7197}{that} \markbox{7198}{the} \markbox{7199}{induced} \markbox{7200}{endomorphisms} \markbox{7201}{in} \markbox{7202}{cohomology} satisfies:
	\begin{enumerate}
		\item {} \markbox{m7203}{$\tilde g^*(c_i)\in uH^*_{\mathbb CG},\forall i\in I$} \markbox{7204}{and} \markbox{m7205}{$\tilde g^*(u)=\mu_1u$} \markbox{7206}{for} \markbox{7207}{some} \markbox{m7208}{$\mu_1\in \mathbb Q$},
		\item {} \markbox{m7209}{$\tilde f$} \markbox{7210}{has} \markbox{7211}{nonzero} Brouwer-degree.
	\end{enumerate}
	\markbox{7212}{Then,} \markbox{7213}{there} \markbox{7214}{is} \markbox{7215}{a} \markbox{7216}{point} \markbox{7217}{of} \markbox{7218}{coincidence} \markbox{7219}{of} \markbox{m7220}{$f$} \markbox{7221}{and}  \markbox{m7222}{$g$}.
\end{proposition}
\fi




\iffalse If \markbox{7223}{we} \markbox{7224}{assume} \markbox{m7225}{$m> 2k$}, \markbox{7226}{then} \markbox{7227}{we} \markbox{7228}{have} \markbox{7229}{more} \markbox{7230}{information} \markbox{7231}{about} \markbox{m7232}{$\tilde f^*$} \markbox{7233}{and} \markbox{7234}{in} \markbox{7235}{that} \markbox{7236}{case} \markbox{7237}{we} \markbox{7238}{don't} \markbox{7239}{have} \markbox{7240}{to} \markbox{7241}{assume} \markbox{7242}{hypothesis} \markbox{7243}{\textit{(2)}}.

We \markbox{7244}{need} \markbox{7245}{to} \markbox{7246}{talk} \markbox{7247}{about} \markbox{7248}{the} \markbox{7249}{similar} \markbox{7250}{situations} \markbox{7251}{when} \markbox{7252}{we} \markbox{7253}{assume} \markbox{7254}{Hoffman} \markbox{7255}{instead} \markbox{7256}{of} Glover-Homer.

We \markbox{7257}{should} \markbox{7258}{be} \markbox{7259}{able} \markbox{7260}{to} \markbox{7261}{find} \markbox{7262}{some} \markbox{7263}{GDS} \markbox{m7264}{$P(m,n,k)$} \markbox{7265}{which} \markbox{7266}{has} FPP.

What \markbox{7267}{happens} \markbox{7268}{if} \markbox{7269}{we} \markbox{7270}{allow} \markbox{m7271}{$m$} \markbox{7272}{to} \markbox{7273}{be} \markbox{7274}{odd} \markbox{7275}{in} \markbox{m7276}{$P(m,n,k)$}?
\fi
